np.nan\n    if end < start: return 0.0\n    # timestamps naive pandas Timestamp\n    total=0.0\n    cur = start.normalize()\n    end_day = end.normalize()\n    one = pd.Timedelta(days=1)\n    while bh_between(start,end):\n    if pd.isna(start) or pd.isna(end) or end<=start: return 0.0\n    total=0.0; cur=start.normalize(); endday=end.normalize(); one=pd.Timedelta(days=1)\n    while {"type":"item.started","item":{"id":"item_34","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"python - <<'PY'\nimport pandas as pd, numpy as np, glob\nWORK_START=9; WORK_END=17\ndef bh(s,e):\n  if pd.isna(s) or pd.isna(e) or e<=s: return 0\n  total=0; cur=s.normalize()\n  while cur<=e.normalize():\n    if cur.weekday()<5:\n      a=max(s,cur+pd.Timedelta(hours=9)); b=min(e,cur+pd.Timedelta(hours=17))\n      if b>a: total+=(b-a).total_seconds()/3600\n    cur+=pd.Timedelta(days=1)\n  return total\nread=lambda p: pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f) for f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/'+p))], ignore_index=True)\nemp=pd.read_csv('/app/employee_001.csv').set_index('employee_id')\ntasks=pd.read_csv('/app/task_001.csv'); assign=read('task_assignment_*.csv'); deps=pd.read_csv('/app/task_dependency_001.csv')\nfor df,cols in [(tasks,['created_at','completed_at']),(assign,['assigned_at','unassigned_at']),(deps,['created_at','resolved_at'])]:\n  for c in cols: df[c]=pd.to_datetime(df[c])\nassign=assign.merge(tasks[['task_id','task_type','priority','complexity_score','risk_score']],on='task_id')\nassign['bh']=[bh(a,b) for a,b in zip(assign.assigned_at,assign.unassigned_at)]\nkey=['assignment_role','task_type','priority']\nmed=assign.groupby(key).bh.transform('median')\nmad=(assign.bh-med).abs().groupby([assign[c] for c in key]).transform('median').replace(0,np.nan)\nassign['z']=(assign.bh-med)/(1.4826*mad)\nassign['excess_bh']=np.maximum(0, assign['bh']-med)\n# dependency overlap with assignments, weighted by z/excess\nrows=[]; abt={tid:g for tid,g in assign.groupby('task_id')}\nfor d in deps.itertuples(index=False):\n  g=abt.get(d.blocking_task_id)\n  if g is None: continue\n  depbh=bh(d.created_at,d.resolved_at)\n  for r in g.itertuples(index=False):\n    ov=bh(max(d.created_at,r.assigned_at), min(d.resolved_at,r.unassigned_at))\n    if ov>0:\n      rows.append((d.dependency_id,d.blocked_task_id,d.blocking_task_id,r.employee_id,r.assignment_role,ov,r.bh,r.z,r.excess_bh,depbh))\nov=pd.DataFrame(rows,columns=['dependency_id','blocked_task_id','blocking_task_id','employee_id','assignment_role','overlap_bh','assign_bh','z','excess_bh','dep_bh'])\nov['weighted_z_overlap']=ov.overlap_bh*ov.z.clip(lower=0)\nov['weighted_excess_overlap']=ov.overlap_bh/ov.assign_bh.replace(0,np.nan)*ov.excess_bh.clip(lower=0)\nagg=ov.groupby('employee_id').agg(dep_count=('dependency_id','nunique'),overlap_bh=('overlap_bh','sum'),wz=('weighted_z_overlap','sum'),wexcess=('weighted_excess_overlap','sum'),max_z=('z','max'),slow_dep_rows=('z',lambda x:(x>3).sum()),extreme_dep_rows=('z',lambda x:(x>10).sum())).join(emp[['role','seniority_level']])\nfor col in ['wz','wexcess','max_z','slow_dep_rows','overlap_bh']:\n print('\\\\nTop',col)\n print(agg.sort_values(col,ascending=False).head(50).round(2).to_string())\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}
